/Users/Mitchell.Sotto/Documents/code/flooranddecorrepos/loyalty-2.0-library/intake/architecture/CARS_Boundary_Systems_Interactions.png ^fVSQ2YjU

Verification
1. user comes through app/ecomm and have
a valid session, want to grant permission.
CARS wants to verify it is a valid session.
JWT check against OKTA accomplishes this.
If a session is not valid, it is rejected by CARS
and the session will have to be refreshed
at the BFF/app level.

2. Enduring long-term permission grants.
If I grant someone the opportunity to use
my account for shipping, free samples, etc.
and these count against me in some way
(using allotment of free stuff), we may want
to ensure that no one is illegally using
my benefits (attribution is not a worry, just
redemption). There needs to be a non-repudiation
signature for the grant given to redeem benefits.
I need to know it came from the person with 
authority to give it (record that it is a valid grant).

Questions
- do we need the security of #2 above in our app?
- does any other system care about that signature
outside of CARS? Would the other apps care? Is there
value in storing the signature? If CARS is the only system doing this, we are
auditing ourselves, which isn't verifiable to be
truthful from another source. ^23uwuXaE
